Message: Direct Invoice Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.invh_no ,to_char( b.invh_cr_dt,'DD/MM/YYYY HH12:MI AM') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.invh_cust_code) as CustName, b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.INVH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.invh_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.INVI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.INVI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.INVI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.INVI_PL_RATE as ItmPrice , a.INVI_QTY as ItmQty, a.INVI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_H_SYS_ID=INVH_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=1 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as totdisamt  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 1000064 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code and  INVH_TXN_CODE='POSINV'

Message: Direct Invoice Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.invh_no ,to_char( b.invh_cr_dt,'DD/MM/YYYY HH12:MI AM') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.invh_cust_code) as CustName, b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.INVH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.invh_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.INVI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.INVI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.INVI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.INVI_PL_RATE as ItmPrice , a.INVI_QTY as ItmQty, a.INVI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_H_SYS_ID=INVH_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=1 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as totdisamt  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 1000072 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code and  INVH_TXN_CODE='POSINV'

Title: 
Message: Direct Invoice Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.invh_no ,to_char( b.invh_cr_dt,'DD/MM/YYYY HH12:MI AM') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.invh_cust_code) as CustName, b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.INVH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.invh_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.INVI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.INVI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.INVI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.INVI_PL_RATE as ItmPrice , a.INVI_QTY as ItmQty, a.INVI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_H_SYS_ID=INVH_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=1 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as totdisamt  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 1000075 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code and  INVH_TXN_CODE='POSINV'

Message: Direct Invoice Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.invh_no ,to_char( b.invh_cr_dt,'DD/MM/YYYY HH12:MI AM') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.invh_cust_code) as CustName, b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.INVH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.invh_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.INVI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.INVI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.INVI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.INVI_PL_RATE as ItmPrice , a.INVI_QTY as ItmQty, a.INVI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_H_SYS_ID=INVH_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=1 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as totdisamt  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 1000078 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code and  INVH_TXN_CODE='POSINV'

Title: 
Message: Direct Invoice Report Query
StackTrace:  select rownum,b.invh_no ,to_char( b.invh_cr_dt,'DD/MM/YYYY HH12:MI AM') as InvoiceDate,  d.ADDR_LINE_1 as locn_name, d.ADDR_LINE_2|| ' ' || d.ADDR_LINE_3 as Location_Address, d.addr_tel as Phone,d.addr_email as Email, (select cust_name from om_customer where cust_code = b.invh_cust_code) as CustName, b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_BILL_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_BILL_COUNTRY_CODE as billing_addr, b.INVH_BILL_TEL as billing_phone, b.invh_BILL_EMAIL as billing_email, b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_1||' '||b.invh_SHIP_ADDR_LINE_2||' '||b.invh_SHIP_COUNTRY_CODE as shipping_addr, a.INVI_ITEM_CODE as ItemCode,a.INVI_ITEM_DESC as ItemDesc, a.INVI_UOM_CODE as ItmUOM, a.INVI_PL_RATE as ItmPrice , a.INVI_QTY as ItmQty, a.INVI_FC_VAL as ItmAmt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as disamt, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_I_SYS_ID=INVI_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=2 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDEXP')),0) as expamt,INVH_SM_CODE as salesman,INVH_FLEX_03 as pmcustno, nvl((select ITED_FC_AMT from OT_INVOICE_ITEM_TED where ITED_H_SYS_ID=INVH_SYS_ID and ITED_TED_HEAD_ITEM_NUM=1 and ITED_TED_TYPE_NUM=(select TED_TAX_DISC_EXP_NUM from OM_TED_TYPE where TED_TYPE_CODE='TEDDIS')),0) as totdisamt  from  ot_invoice_head b,ot_invoice_item a,om_location c,om_address d where b.invh_no = 1000082 and b.invh_sys_id = a.invi_invh_sys_id and b.invh_locn_code = c.locn_code and c.locn_addr_code = d.addr_code and  INVH_TXN_CODE='POSINV'
